CIRCUMSTANCES.\n  THE FLIGHT PLANS WILL BE FILLED ACCORDINGLY.\n<b>A6167/23   </b>\n  OPERATIONS IN FLIGHT INFORMATION REGIONS\n  ONGOING MILITARY ACTIVITY IN UKRAINE AND ALONG THE BORDER OF\n  UKRAINE/RUSSIA AND USE OF A WIDE RANGE OF GROUND AND AIRBORNE\n  WARFARE SYSTEMS POSES A HIGH RISK FOR CIVIL FLIGHTS OPERATING\n  AT ALL ALTITUDES AND FLIGHT LEVELS.\n  ROMANIAN AIR OPERATORS AND OWNERS OF ACFT REGISTERED IN ROMANIA\n  ARE ADVISED NOT TO ENTER FIL LVIV (UKLV), FIR KYIV (UKBV),\n  FIR DNIPROPETROVSK (UKDV), FIR SIMFEROPOL (UKFV),\n  FIR ODESA (UKOV), FIR ROSTOV (URRV) AND TO TAKE ALL POTENTIAL\n  RISK INTO ACCOUNT IN RISK ASSESSMENT AND FLIGHT PLANNING\n  DECISIONS WHEN OPERATING 200NM SURROUNDING THE BORDERS WITH\n  UKRAINE IN THE FIR MOSCOW (UUWW) AND FIR ROSTOV (URRV).\n<b>A6166/23   </b>\n  ANY AIRCRAFT OPERATED BY AN AIR TRANSPORT UNDERTAKING HOLDING\n  A VALID OPERATING LICENCE OR EQUIVALENT ISSUED BY THE COMPETENT\n  AUTHORITIES OF BELARUS, INCLUDING AS A MARKETING CARRIER IN\n  CODE-SHARING OR BLOCKED-SPACE ARRANGEMENTS, ARE PROHIBITED TO\n  TAKE OFF FROM, LAND IN OR OVERFLY THE ROMANIAN TERRITORY EXCEPT\n  IN THE CASE OF AN EMERGENCY LANDING OR AN EMERGENCY OVERFLIGHT.<h2 style=\"page-break-after: always;\"> </h2><b>A5567/23   </b>\n  FLIGHT RESTRICTIONS\n  MILITARY INVASION OF UKRAINE BY RUSSIAN FEDERATION - ROMANIAN\n  AIR OPERATORS AND OWNERS OF AIRCRAFT REGISTERED IN ROMANIA SHALL\n  NOT ENTER FIR KYIV (UKBU), FIR LVIV (UKLV), FIR KYIV (UKBV),\n  FIR DNIPROPETROVSK (UKDV), FIR SIMFEROPOL (UKFV), FIR ODESA\n  (UKOV), FIR ROSTOV-NA-DONU (URRV).\n  SAID OPERATORS AND AICRAFT OWNERS SHALL ALSO AVOID FLIGHT\n  OPERATIONS WITHIN THE BUFFER ZONE EXTENDING OUT TO 200NM ALONG\n  THE UKRAINE/RUSSIA BORDER.\n  OPERATIONS WITHIN THE FIR CHISINAU (LUUU) AIRSPACE SHALL ONLY\n  BE UNDERTAKEN IN COMPLIANCE WITH APPLICABLE AERONAUTICAL\n  PUBLICATIONS ISSUED BY REPUBLIC OF MOLDOVA.\n  OPERATORS ARE REMINDED THAT OPERATIONS WITHIN FIR MINSK (UMMV)\n  ARE PROHIBITED IN ACCORDANCE WITH EASA SAFETY DIRECTIVES\n  SD-2021-02 AND SD-2021-03.\n  ADDITIONAL RISK ASSESSMENT AND FLIGHT PLANNING DECISIONS SHALL\n  BE TAKEN BEFORE OPERATING IN THE FOLLOWING AIRSPACE:\n  MOSCOW (UUWV\n<b>A5568/23   </b>\n  GNSS OUTAGE:\n  OCCASIONALLY GNSS SIGNAL JAMMING AND/OR POSSIBLE SPOOFING WERE\n  ENCOUNTERED AND REPORTED BY AIRCRAFT OVERFLYING BUCURESTI FIR.\n  AIRCREWS SHALL EXERCISE <b>CAUTION</b> WHEN USING FLIGHT NAVIGATION\n  BASED ON THESE SENSORS IN DIFFERENT PHASES OF THE FLIGHT. IN\n  BUCURESTI FIR CONVENTIONAL NAVIGATION INFRASTRUCTURE <b>AVAILABLE</b>.\n  FOR MORE INFORMATION, PLEASE ALSO CONSULT EASA SIB NO. 2022-02R2.\n<b>A5566/23   </b>\n  FLIGHT RESTRICTIONS.\n  UKRAINIAN CRISIS - ALL RUSSIAN REGISTERED AIRCRAFT AND AIRCRAFT\n  OWNED, CHARTERED OR OPERATED BY NATURAL OR LEGAL PERSONS FROM\n  THE RUSSIAN FEDERATION OR BY OPERATORS HOLDING AIR OPERATOR\n  CERTIFICATE (AOC) ISSUED BY THE RUSSIAN FEDERATION AUTHORITIES\n  ARE PROHIBITED TO ENTER, EXIT OR OVERFLY ROMANIAN AIRSPACE\n  EXCEPT HUMANITARIAN, SAR AND LEASED AIRCRAFT ONE-WAY RETURN\n  FLIGHTS FIR/UIR ++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++\n\n<b>A6758/23   </b>\n  MILITARY INVASION OF UKRAINE BY RUSSIAN FEDERATION\n  ONGOING MILITARY ACTIVITY IN UKRAINE AND THE AIRSPACE WITHIN 200NM\n  ALONG BORDER UKRAINE/RUSSIA IN THE MOSCOW FIR USE OF A WIDE RANGE\n  OF GROUND AND AIRBORNE WARFARE SYSTEMS WHICH POSE A HIGH RISK FOR\n  CIVIL FLIGHTS OPERATING AT ALL ALTITUDES AND FLIGHT LEVELS.\n  AIR CARRIERS HOLDING OPERATING LICENCE ISSUED BY HUNGARY - PILOTS\n  IN COMMAND OF ACFT CONDUCTING AIR SERVICES BY HUNGARIAN OPERATING\n  LICENCE HOLDERS AND OPERATORS OF HUNGARIAN REGISTERED ACFT\n  SHALL NOT ENTER FIR LVIV (UKLV), FIR KYIV (UKBV), UIR KYIV (UKBU),\n  FIR DNIPROPETROVSK (UKDV), FIR SIMFEROPOL (UKFV), FIR ODESA\n  (UKOV), FIR ROSTOV-NA-DONU (URRV). SAID OPERATORS AND AIRCRAFT\n  OWNERS SHALL ALSO AVOID FLIGHT OPERATIONS WITHIN THE BUFFER ZONE\n  EXTENDING OUT TO 200NM ALONG THE UKRAINE/RUSSIA BORDER. OPERATIONS\n  WITHIN THE FIR CHISNAU (LUUU) AIRSPACE SHALL ONLY BE UNDERTAKEN IN\n  COMPLIENCE WITH APPLICABLE AERONAUTICAL PUBLICATIONS ISSUED BY\n  REPUBLIC OF MOLDOVA. ADDITIONAL RISK ASSESSMENT AND FLIGHT\n  PLANNING DECISIONS SHALL BE TAKEN BEFORE OPERATING IN FOLLOWING\n  AIRSPACE: MOSCOW (UUWV).\n<b>A6741/23   </b>\n  MILITARY INVASION OF UKRAINE BY RUSSIAN FEDERATION\n  ALL RUSSIAN REGISTERED AIRCRAFT AND ALL AIRCRAFT OWNED, CHARTERED\n  OR OPERATED BY ANY RUSSIAN NATURAL OR LEGAL PERSON, OPERATORS\n  HOLDING OPERATING LICENCE (OL) OR EQUIVALENT ISSUED BY THE RUSSIAN\n  FEDERATION AUTHORITIES, INCLUDING AS A MARKETING CARRIER ARE\n  PROHIBITED TO ENTER, EXIT OR OVERFLY HUNGARIAN AIRSPACE EXCEPT\n  HUMANITARIAN, SAR AND LEASED AIRCRAFT ONE-WAY RETURN FLIGHTS WITH\n  THE PERMISSION OF THE HUNGARIAN CAA AND IN CASE OF EMERGENCY\n  LANDING OR EMERGENCY OVERFLIGHT.\n<b>A6659/23   </b>\n  AIR CARRIERS HOLDING OPERATING LICENCE ISSUED BY HUNGARY - PILOTS \n  IN COMMAND OF ACFT CONDUCTING AIR SERVICES BY HUNGARIAN OPERATING\n  LICENCE HOLDERS AND OPERATORS OF HUNGARIAN REGISTERED ACFT ARE NOT\n  PERMITTED TO ENTER MINSK FIR (UMMV) UNLESS THE USE OF THAT\n  AIRSPACE IS DEEMED NECESSARY TO ENSURE SAFE OPERATION IN CASE OF\n  UNFORESEEN CIRCUMSTANCES. FOREIGN AIR CARRIERS INBOUND AND\n  OUTBOUND EU ARE RECOMMENDED TO AVOID BELARUS MINSK FIR (UMMV).\n<b>A6658/23   </b>\n  ALL FLIGHTS TO/FROM AIRPORTS OF HUNGARY, OR OVERFLYING HUNGARIAN \n  TERRITORY, ARE NOT ALLOWED IF AIRCRAFT ARE OPERATED BY BELARUSSIAN\n  AIR CARRIERS AND/OR REGISTRATED IN BELARUS AND/OR INCLUDED IN THE\n  REG EC NO 765/2006 EXCEPT FOR AIRCRAFT IN EMERGENCY OR\n  HUMANITARIAN FLIGHTS.\n<b>A5541/23   </b>\n  HUNGARIAN ATC SERVICE IS NOT ELIGIBLE TO GIVE ENTRY OR CROSSING \n  CLEARENCE INTO THE UKRAINE AIRSPACE IN ANY CIRCUMSTANCES (E.G.\n  DURING THUNDERSTORM AVOIDING ACTION) UNLESS AIRCRAFT IS EXEMPTED\n  ACCORDING TO NOTAM REF NUMBER A0089/23 ISSUED BY UKKR NOF.\n  HUNGARIAN ATS AND SEARCH AND RESCUE IS PROVIDED ONLY WITHIN\n  BUDAPEST FIR. PILOTS MAY\n  EITHER SELECT A SPECIFIC COST INDEX NUMBER FROM THE LIST, OR THEY\n  MAY SELECT \"AUTO\". WHEN PLANNING AN \"AUTO\" COST INDEX, THE SYSTEM\n  WILL REFERENCE THE SCHEDULED \"TIME ENROUTE\" OPTION AND ATTEMPT TO\n  CHOOSE A COST INDEX WHICH CLOSELY MATCHES THIS VALUE. NOTE THAT\n  THE \"TIME ENROUTE\" OPTION IS MEANT AS A GATE TO GATE TIME (AS\n  INDICATED ON AN AIRLINE'S FLIGHT SCHEDULE, FOR EXAMPLE). IF A\n  \"TIME ENROUTE\" OF 2:30 IS SELECTED, THE SYSTEM WILL SUBTRACT THE\n  TAXI TIMES FROM THIS VALUE TO DETERMINE THE SCHEDULED AIR TIME. IT\n  WILL THEN DETERMINE AND USE THE COST INDEX WHICH MATCHES THIS AIR\n  TIME.\n\n<b>SB003/13   </b>\n  SUBJECT: FLIGHT RELEASE UNITS\n  ALL FLIGHT CREW: PLEASE PAY SPECIAL ATTENTION TO THE UNITS\n  SELECTION WHEN GENERATING A FLIGHT PLAN.
